🛑 18,791 government schools in Karnataka have no land records
--------------------
**18,791 government schools in Karnataka lack official land records.** This indicates a vast number of state-run educational institutions operate without proper legal documentation of their property.
*   The absence of these records means **their land ownership is not formally registered or documented**, which can lead to legal ambiguities.
*   This situation poses **significant challenges for legal clarity, potential future development, and the overall security** of these school properties.

Source: https://www.thehindu.com/news/national/karnataka/18791-government-schools-in-karnataka-have-no-land-records/article70610529.ece

🛑 On India’s fighter jet acquisitions
--------------------
Here are 3 bullet points summarizing the topic "On India's fighter jet acquisitions":

*   **Modernization and Security Needs:** India's ongoing efforts to upgrade its air force to counter regional threats, maintain air superiority, and replace aging fleets.
*   **Blend of Foreign and Indigenous Sourcing:** The country pursues a strategy of acquiring advanced jets from international partners (e.g., France, Russia, USA) while simultaneously emphasizing domestic manufacturing and technology transfer under initiatives like 'Make in India'.
*   **Strategic and Geopolitical Impact:** These acquisitions involve significant financial outlays, complex negotiations, and have broader implications for India's strategic partnerships, defence industrial base, and its role in the regional power balance.
